A dictionary of terms in the [[Low Alöbi]] language.

# a
### -a

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-a|*-a]]_.
> ¹ Adjunct
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-a|-a]]_ ("adjective")
### abta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑbtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑbdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [abda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*apta|*apta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Laid out flat; ² Arranged in a particular way
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#abda|abda]]_
### acas
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑtʃɑs]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒɑs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒas]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*acas|*acas]]_.
> ¹ Snake
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ajas|ajas]]_
### acok'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑtʃokʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒɔkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒɔkʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*acuk'|*acuk']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cuq'|*cuq']]_ ("stone").
> ¹ Stone
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ajok|ajok]]_
### acowmö
ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒowmœ]

*num.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#acö|acö]]_ ("one") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#omö|omö]]_ ("five").
> ¹ Six
### acö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑtʃø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʒœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʒœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔacü|*ʔacü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔac|*ʔac]]_ ("one").
> ¹ One
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#acowmö|acowmö]]_ ("six")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#újö|újö]]_
### -ag

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ag|*-ag]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count smaller land animals that are typically considered edible such as [[K'übi]], flightless birds and big toads
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-on|-on]]_
### agök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑŋøk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aŋœk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*agük|*agük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ag|*ag]]_ ("open") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ük|*ük]]_ ("split").
> ¹ To split open
### agta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑɴtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑndɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*agta|*agta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ag|*ag]]_ ("open") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Opened up, as of a flower
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#anda|anda]]_
### aib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ayip|*ayip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ip|*ip]]_ ("thin, narrow").
> ¹ Narrow gap
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#eb|eb]]_
### aigem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑiŋem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjŋɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajŋɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ayīgem|*ayīgem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īg|*īg]]_ ("enter") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Entrance; ² Door
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#egen|egen]]_
### ainklos
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑinklos]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑɪ̃ŋklɔs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajŋklɔs]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ayinqrus|*ayinqrus]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*inqrus|*inqrus]]_ ("the sun").
> ¹ Sunlight
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#enklos|enklos]]_
### akyaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑkjɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑkjɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [akjaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*akyaw|*akyaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyaw|*kyaw]]_ ("scream").
> ¹ To screech, caw; ² To scream, call out
### alig
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑliŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑlɪ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [alɪ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔalīg|*ʔalīg]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔal-|*ʔal-]]_ ("outside, outer") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*īg|*īg]]_ ("enter").
> ¹ To exit a building, cave or other enclosed space
### alt'ak'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑltʼɑqʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑɫtʼɑqʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [awtʼaqʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔalt'aq'|*ʔalt'aq']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔal-|*ʔal-]]_ ("outside, outer") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'aq'|*t'aq']]_ ("shell").
> ¹ Shell of an animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#otak|otak]]_
### ama
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑmɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ama]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔama|*ʔama]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔam|*ʔam]]_ ("more").
> ¹ Bigger than
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ama|ama]]_
### amam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑmɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [amam]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*amam|*amam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*am|*am]]_ ("house") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Hut
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#aman|aman]]_
### amel
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmel]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑmɛɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [amew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*amwer|*amwer]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*am-|*am-]]_ ("comparative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wer|*wer]]_ ("measure").
> ¹ To compare to; ² To weigh
### amkis
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkis]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋkɪs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aŋkɪs]

> ¹ To be above
### amküc'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkytʃʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋkʏtʃʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aŋkʏtʃʼ]

### amk'i
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkʼi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋkʼɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aŋkʼɪ]

ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑmkʼøj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑŋkʼœj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aŋkʼej]

### amök'

### amöt

> ¹ To be exactly equal to; ² To be roughly equivalent to
### ana
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑnɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ana]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*anaʔ|*anaʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naq|*naq]]_ ("eat").
> ¹ To eat
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#anaqa|anaqa]]_ ("mouth, opening")
### anaqa
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnɑʔɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anaʔa]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#ana|ana]]_ ("to eat"). Perhaps related to [[Low Alöbi]] _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#kiaq|kiaq]]_ ("to bite"), [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#na’a|na’a]]_ ("mouth").
> ¹ Mouth, opening
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ana|ana]]_
### anök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑnøk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anœk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*anük|*anük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ük|*ük]]_ ("split").
> ¹ Axe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#anök|anök]]_
### anxub
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑnʃub]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑnʃʊb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [anʃʊb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*anxūp|*anxūp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xūp|*xūp]]_ ("adze").
> ¹ Adze, a tool used to hollow out a log into a canoe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#anxub|anxub]]_
### aqaq
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑʔɑʔ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑʔɑʔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aʔaʔ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*aqaq|*aqaq]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*aq|*aq]]_ ("bite, chew") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("repetitively").
> ¹ To chew
### atüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑtym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑdʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [adʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*atyǖm|*atyǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyǖm|*tyǖm]]_ ("pouch, pocket").
> ¹ Pouch, pocket
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#adun|adun]]_
### aül
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑyl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑʏɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aew]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔayǖr|*ʔayǖr]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔǖr|*ʔǖr]]_ ("night").
> ¹ Nighttime
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#aülinklos|aülinklos]]_ ("nighttime sun")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ö|ö]]_
### aülinklos
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑylinklos]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑʏlɪ̃ŋklɔs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [aʏlɪ̃ŋklɔs]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#aül|aül]]_ ("nighttime") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#inklos|inklos]]_ ("the sun").
> ¹ The nighttime sun, a name for [[Bigmoon]] in its full phase
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ölinklos|ölinklos]]_
### awa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [awa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*agwa|*agwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ag|*ag]]_ ("open") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Open, as of a mouth or cave
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ova|ova]]_
### awi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑwi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑwɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [awɪ]

### -ay

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ay|*-ay]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count pieces of a segmental structure such as teeth, scales, words and units of time
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-e|-e]]_
### ayag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjɑɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajaɴ]

### ayamem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjɑmem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjɑmɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajamɛ̃ː]

### aylib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjlib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjlɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajlɪb]

### ayom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajɔ̃ː]

> ¹ Outdoors; ² Forest
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#eyon|eyon]]_
### aywam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ɑjwɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɑjwɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ajwam]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔaywam|*ʔaywam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔwam|*ʔwam]]_ ("firmament").
> ¹ The celestial sphere, the surface on which the stars and celestial bodies lie
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#evan|evan]]_
# b
### babay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑbɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑbɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [babaj]

> ¹ Layer; ² Coating
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#babe|babe]]_
### bac'ük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑtʃʼyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑtʃʼʏk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [batʃʼʏk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pac'ǖk|*pac'ǖk]]_.
> ¹ To break
### bamay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑmɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑmɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bamaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pamay|*pamay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pa-|*pa-]]_ ("gather or obtain") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*may|*may]]_ ("know, remember").
> ¹ To research, gather knowledge; ² To develop an understanding
### bamit
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑmit]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑmɪt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bamɪt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pamīt|*pamīt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pamay|*pamay]]_ ("to research") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Knowledge
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#bamit|bamit]]_
### banat'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑnɑtʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑnɑtʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [banatʼ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*panat'|*panat']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pat'|*pat']]_ ("colour").
> ¹ Dye, pigment powder
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#banat|banat]]_
### banban
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑnbɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑmbɑn]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bamban]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*panpan|*panpan]]_.
> ¹ A sweet fruit
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#banban|banban]]_
### banis
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑnis]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑnɪs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [banɪs]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*panis|*panis]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pa-|*pa-]]_ ("gather or obtain") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nis|*nis]]_ ("sense physically").
> ¹ To sense, physically feel
### banö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑnø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑnœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [banœ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*panü|*panü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pa-|*pa-]]_ ("gather or obtain") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nü|*nü]]_ ("see").
> ¹ To see
### banöt
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑnøt]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑnœt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [banœt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*panüt|*panüt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*püt|*püt]]_ ("paint").
> ¹ Paintbrush
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#banöt|banöt]]_
### banta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑntɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑndɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [banda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pwanta|*pwanta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pwan|*pwan]]_ ("fill") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Full
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#banda|banda]]_
### banya
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑɲɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑɲɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [baɲa]

> ¹ To hear
### batko
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑtko]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑtkɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [batkɔ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*patku|*patku]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pat'|*pat']]_ ("colour") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ku|*-ku]]_ ("-ness").
> ¹ Colour, hue
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#batko|batko]]_
### baü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [baj]

> ¹ Tree
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#be|be]]_
### bawö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑwø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑwœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bawœ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pawü|*pawü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wüʔ|*wüʔ]]_ ("omen, luck").
> ¹ Omen
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#bovö|bovö]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#paweu|paweu]]_
### baya
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑjɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑjɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [baja]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*payyaʔ|*payyaʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pyaʔ|*pyaʔ]]_ ("random, erratic").
> ¹ Random or unexpected event; ² Anomaly
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#beya|beya]]_
### bayal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bɑjɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɑjɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bajaw]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*payal|*payal]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pal|*pal]]_ ("wax, flow, accumulate").
> ¹ The first half of a _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#omö|omö]]_
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#beyo|beyo]]_
### bibat'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bibɑtʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bibɑtʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bibatʼ]

> ¹ To colour, dye
### bibix
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bibiʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bibɪʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bibɪʃ]

> ¹ To varnish; ² To polish
### bic'ip'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bitʃʼipʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bitʃʼɪpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bitʃʼɪpʼ]

### bigbig
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [biŋbiŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bɪ̃mbɪ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bɪ̃mbɪ̃ː]

### bigi

> ¹ To carry; ² To bear the weight of
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#bígi|bígi]]_ ("to bear")
### bik'i
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bikʼi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bikʼɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bikʼɪ]

> ¹ To hang onto
### bilbil
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bilbil]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [biɫbɪɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bewbew]

### bilis

### bilüc

### binbin

### binem

### böta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [bøtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [bødɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [bøda]

### bötböt

### bötic

### cik'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃikʼem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃikʼɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃikʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīk'em|*cīk'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cīk'|*cīk']]_ ("tip") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Tail; ² Back end
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jíken|jíken]]_
### cimcim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃimtʃim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃɪ̃ndʒɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃɪ̃ndʒɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cimcim|*cimcim]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ci|*ci]]_ ("red") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ [[Cimcim]], edible red algae cultivated by the Öb
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jinjin|jinjin]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#cimcim|cimcim]]_
### cisk'on
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃiskʼon]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃiskʼɔ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃiskʼɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cisk'un|*cisk'un]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ci|*ci]]_ ("red") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sek'u|*sek'u]]_ ("beak") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-en|*-en]]_ ("possessed").
> ¹ [[Cisk'on]], a species of kingfisher with a red beak
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jískon|jískon]]_
### cita
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʃitɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʃidɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʃida]

> ¹ To have passed
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jída|jída]]_
### clogi

### colan

### c'abet

> ¹ Human singular
### eal

ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilbu]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋiɫbʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewbʊ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilpū|*gilpū]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pū|*pū]]_ ("elder sibling").
> ¹ The larger of the two moons of winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#göbu|göbu]]_
### gilki
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilki]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋiɫkɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewkɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilki|*gilki]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ki|*ki]]_ ("younger sibling").
> ¹ The smaller of the two moons of winter
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#göki|göki]]_
### gilmö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋilmø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋiɫmœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋewmœ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gilmü|*gilmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gil|*gil]]_ ("moon") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A minor month, equal to 10 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gömö|gömö]]_
### gosum
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋosum]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋosʊ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋosʊ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gusūm|*gusūm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sūm|*sūm]]_ ("remove").
> ¹ To remove
### gük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ŋyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ŋyk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ŋyk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gǖk|*gǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gaw|*gaw]]_ ("north-easterly wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ North-easterly wind
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#gík|gík]]_
# h
### habom
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑbom]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑbɔ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χabɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To ripen
### haim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χaj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hayīm|*hayīm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hüy|*hüy]]_ ("rest") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Bed; ² Bedroom, personal quarters
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#he|he]]_
### hamog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To keep trying, working towards something
### hamök'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøkʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamœkʼ]

> ¹ To grow old
### hamök'et
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøkʼet]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœkʼɛt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamœkʼɛt]

> ¹ Old person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#hanket|hanket]]_
### hamöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hamül|*hamül]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ha-|*ha-]]_ ("progressive") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mül|*mül]]_ ("learn, teach").
> ¹ To develop a skill; ² To learn something
### hamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To grow; ² To develop
### hamöx
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [χɑmøʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [χɑmœʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [χamœʃ]

### hanim

### hia

### hilap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [xilɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [xilɑpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [xilapʼ]

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#hílap|hílap]]_
### hiwhiw

> ¹ To breathe
### hiwmö

### holaq

*v.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#fara’e|fara’e]]_ ("to burn, cook"), from _[[Xiri dictionary#fa-|fa-]]_ ("verb prefix") + _[[Xiri dictionary#rha’e|rha’e]]_ ("fire").
> ¹ To cook

### honu

*v.* Perhaps related to [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#furu|furu]]_ ("to make, mold").
> ¹ To create
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#honuta|honuta]]_ ("artificial")
### honuta
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɸonʊdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɸonʊda]

### hoqaw
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɸoʔɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɸoʔaw]

### höe
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [xʷøe]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɸøɛ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɸøə]

> ¹ A yellow flower which grows on the branches of a certain tree species

### hyac'ek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [çɑtʃʼek]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɕɑtʃʼɛk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɕatʃʼɛk]

### iba

### ica

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íja|íja]]_
### icab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒab]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔicap|*ʔicap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ʔic|*ʔic]]_ ("wide, broad") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ap|*ap]]_ ("lay out, arrange").
> ¹ To lay out flat; ² To position far apart
### icaqa
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [idʒɑʔɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [idʒaʔa]

*stat.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#ici|ici]]_ ("pig").
> ¹ Fat, as of a person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#íca|íca]]_
### ichamön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃχɑmøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [itʃχɑmœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [itʃχamɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To grow, as of a plant
### ici

### icköc
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [itʃkøtʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [itʃkœtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [itʃkœtʃ]

### ic'ik'

### kagkag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qɑɴqɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qɑɴqɑɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qaɴqaɴ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kaŋkaŋ|*kaŋkaŋ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kaŋ|*kaŋ]]_ ("boil, brew") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Soup, stew
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kankan|kankan]]_
### kaig
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qɑiŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qɑɪ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qaj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kayig|*kayig]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kig|*kig]]_ ("excrement").
> ¹ Intestines
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ke|ke]]_
### kale
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qɑlɛ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qalə]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#kare|kare]]_ ("demon"), from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*kale|*kale]]_.
> ¹ Demon, evil spirit
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kala|kala]]_
### kanöc'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qɑnøtʃʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qɑnœtʃʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qanœtʃʼ]

### katam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qɑtɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qɑdɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qadam]

### kat'un

### küc'a
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kytʃʼɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kytʃʼɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kytʃʼa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kǖc'a|*kǖc'a]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kǖc'|*kǖc']]_ ("high").
> ¹ High up, as of a cliff or cloud; ² Far down
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíca|kíca]]_
### kük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kyk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kyk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwǖk|*qwǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwiw|*qwiw]]_ ("south-easterly monsoon wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ South-easterly monsoon wind
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kík|kík]]_
### kükü
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kykʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kykʏ]

*n.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#kwi|kwi]]_ ("yam"), from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*kue|*kue]]_.
> ¹ Tuber; ² Yam
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#cikü|cikü]]_ ("red potato")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíkö|kíkö]]_
### kwilta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kwiltɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kwiɫdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kwewda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kwilta|*kwilta]]_, Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kil|*kil]]_ ("tired, bored").
> ¹ Lazy
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#köda|köda]]_
### kyahyac'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑçɑtʃʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑɕɑtʃʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjaɕatʃʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyahyac'|*kyahyac']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*hyac'|*hyac']]_ ("jump").
> ¹ To jump; ² To spring forward
### kyakop'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑkopʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑkɔpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjakɔpʼ]

> ¹ To burst
### kyak'ay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑqʼɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑqʼɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjaqʼaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyaq'ay|*kyaq'ay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kya-|*kya-]]_ ("suddenly or accidentally") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'ay|*q'ay]]_ ("fall").
> ¹ To fall off; ² To fall over; ³ To collapse
### kyak'öb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑkʼøb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑkʼœb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjakʼœb]

> ¹ To vomit
### kyalap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑlɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑlɑpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjalapʼ]

> ¹ To snatch
### kyalwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑlwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑɫwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawwa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyalwa|*kyalwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyal|*kyal]]_ ("lay") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Laying flat on the ground
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyova|kyova]]_
### kyanem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑnem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑnɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjanɛ̃ː]

> ¹ Hat
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyanen|kyanen]]_
### kyanit
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑnit]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑnɪt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjanɪt]

> ¹ Idea
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyanit|kyanit]]_
### kyanta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑntɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑndɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjanda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qyanta|*qyanta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qyan|*qyan]]_ ("cover") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kyanda|kyanda]]_
### kyat'ay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑtʼɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑtʼɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjatʼaj]

> ¹ To disappear
### kyawih
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑwix]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑwx]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawx]

### kyawik'

> ¹ To change (suddenly or unexpectedly)
### kyawkyaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kjɑwkjɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kjɑwkjɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kjawkjaw]

> ¹ To caw, howl
# k'
### k'abah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbɑχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼabaχ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'apah|*q'apah]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'a|*q'a]]_ ("peak").
> ¹ The mountains of [[T'ugü]]'
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'abahcüw|k'abahcüw]]_ ("öxp'a")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kabah|kabah]]_
### k'abahcüw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbɑχtʃyw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbɑχtʃʏw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼabaχtʃew]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'abah|k'abah]]_ ("mountains") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#cüw|cüw]]_ ("cüo").
> ¹ A large wug, similar to terrestrial takin
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kabahcö|kabahcö]]_
### k'abk'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑbqʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑbqʼɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼabqʼab]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'apk'ap|*k'apk'ap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ap|*k'ap]]_ ("sea mollusc") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Any sea mollusc with an external shell
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kapkab|kapkab]]_

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'apk'ap|*k'apk'ap]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ap|*k'ap]]_ ("sweat") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To sweat
### k'ak'ohümi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑkʼoxʷymi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑkʼɔɸʏmɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼakʼɔɸʏmɪ]

*n.* From [[High Alöbi]] _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ugǖmi|q'aq'ugǖmi]]_, from _[[High Alöbi dictionary#q'aq'ug|q'aq'ug]]_ ("giant snail") + _[[High Alöbi dictionary#ǖm|ǖm]]_ ("wooden construction") + _[[High Alöbi dictionary#-i|-i]]_ ("relational linker"). Equivalent to _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#t'ak'og|t'ak'og]]_ ("giant snail") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üm|üm]]_ ("wooden construction") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#-i|-i]]_ ("relational linker").
> ¹ A large wagon which can be inverted to form a temporary home, used in [[Öb#Seasonal migration|Öb seasonal migrations]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kakofmi|kakofmi]]_
### k'atbaü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑtbɑy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑdbɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼadbaj]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'atpaǖ|*k'atpaǖ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'at|*k'at]]_ ("base, bottom part") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*paǖ|*paǖ]]_ ("tree").
> ¹ Tree trunk, stump
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kadbe|kadbe]]_
### k'atem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [qʼɑtem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [qʼɑdɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [qʼadɛ̃ː]

### k'ic'og

### k'ilunön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼilunøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiɫnœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼewnɔ̃ː]

> ¹ A spice made from the root of the [[K'unön]] plant
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#könon|könon]]_
### k'imaq
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼimɑʔ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼimɑʔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼimaʔ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'imaq|*k'imaq]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i-|*k'i-]]_ ("again") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*maq|*maq]]_ ("repeat").
> ¹ To repeat; ² To try again
### k'imay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼimɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼimɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼimaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'imay|*k'imay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i-|*k'i-]]_ ("again") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*may|*may]]_ ("know, remember").
> ¹ To remember
### k'iwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼiwa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'iwa|*k'iwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i|*k'i]]_ ("hang, swing") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Hanging
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíva|kíva]]_
### k'iwk'iw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiwkʼiw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiwkʼɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼewkʼew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'iwk'iw|*k'iwk'iw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'iw|*k'iw]]_ ("cry") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To cry
### k'ixam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼiʃɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼiʃɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼiʃam]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ixam|*k'ixam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*xam|*xam]]_ ("throw").
> ¹ Spear
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíxan|kíxan]]_
### k'lablix
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼlɑbliʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼlɑblɪʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼlablɪʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'laplix|*k'laplix]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'lap'|*q'lap']]_ ("lightning, thunder") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'atlix|*p'atlix]]_ ("bright flash of light").
> ¹ Electrical storm; ² Lightning strike
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#klablix|klablix]]_
### k'unön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼunøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼunœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼunɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ūnün|*k'ūnün]]_.
> ¹ A plant whose roots are used to make the spice [[K'unön#K'ilunön|k'ilunön']]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kúnon|kúnon]]_
### k'übi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼybi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼybɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼybɪ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'ǖpi|*k'ǖpi]]_.
> ¹ [[K'übi]], a small domesticated ungulate kept as livestock, similar to duikers
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kíbi|kíbi]]_
### k'winta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼwintɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼwɪ̃ndɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼwɪ̃nda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'winta|*q'winta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'win|*q'win]]_ ("dark") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Dark; ² Dull, blunt
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kvinda|kvinda]]_
### k'winwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [kʼwinwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [kʼwimɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [kʼwima]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'winwa|*q'winwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'win|*q'win]]_ ("dark") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Dark
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#kvíma|kvíma]]_
# l
### labet
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑbet]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑbɛt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [labɛt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rapet|*rapet]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rap|*rap]]_ ("bind, restrain") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Bundle (of sticks); ² Clump of bamboo
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#labet|labet]]_
### labina
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑbinɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑbɪnɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [labɪna]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rapina|*rapina]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pin|*pin]]_ ("bitter").
> ¹ Bitter; ² Unripe
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#labna|labna]]_
### lablah
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑblɑχ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑblɑχ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lablaχ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*glaplah|*glaplah]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*glap|*glap]]_ ("star cluster").
> ¹ The dense cluster of stars at the core of the globular cluster
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lablah|lablah]]_
### laibem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑibem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑjbɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lajbɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*layipem|*layipem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lip|*lip]]_ ("trap") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Pitfall trap
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#leben|leben]]_
### lakawa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑqɑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑqɑwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [laqawa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rakawa|*rakawa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kaw|*kaw]]_ ("urine").
> ¹ Smelling of urine
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lakva|lakva]]_
### lakig
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑkiŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑkɪ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lakɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rakig|*rakig]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kig|*kig]]_ ("excrement").
> ¹ Smell of excrement
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lakin|lakin]]_
### lakwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑkwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑkwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lakwa]

> ¹ Foul-smelling
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lakva|lakva]]_
### lak'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑkʼem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑkʼɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lakʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lak'em|*lak'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lak'|*lak']]_ ("insert") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Plug, cork
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#laken|laken]]_
### -lam

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-lam|*-lam]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count flat, stackable objects such as flatbreads, leaves and pieces of cloth
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-lon|-lon]]_
### lamüa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑmyɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑmʏɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lamʏa]

### lanog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑnoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑnɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lanɔ̃ː]

### laqaka
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑʔɑqɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑʔɑqɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [laʔaqa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raqaka|*raqaka]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ra|*ra]]_ ("smell, taste") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qak|*qak]]_ ("putrid").
> ¹ Putrid
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#laka|laka]]_, [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#rha’aga|rha’aga]]_
### laqem
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑʔɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [laʔɛ̃ː]

> ¹ Cooked food
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#laqen|laqen]]_
### laqtaqa

### latoga

### latüxa

### lat'aga

### laüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [law]

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lo|lo]]_
### lawic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lɑwitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɑwtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lawtʃ]

### laxöw

### lib

### lihas

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#líhas|líhas]]_
### lihwel

### lik

### lilaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lilɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lilɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lilaw]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*rilaw|*rilaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<il>|*<il>]]_ ("result or product") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raw|*raw]]_ ("sew, weave").
> ¹ Linen cloth
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lílo|lílo]]_ ("cloth, sail") → [[Ahōtoli]] _[[Ahōtoli dictionary#lilō|lilō]]_ ("sail of a ship")
### lim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [lim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [lɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [lɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*līm|*līm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lay|*lay]]_ ("all, every") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Everything
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#lin|lin]]_
### lisem

### liswin

### lökic

### mawso
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mɑwso]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mɑwsɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [mawsɔ]

*pron.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mawsu|*mawsu]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ma-|*ma-]]_ ("human paucal") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*usu|*usu]]_ ("second person").
> ¹ Second person paucal
### mayaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mɑjɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mɑjɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [majaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mayaw|*mayaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ma-|*ma-]]_ ("inside, inner") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("enclose").
> ¹ To enclose
### mayot'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mɑjotʼem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mɑjtʼɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [majtʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*maywit'em|*maywit'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mwit'|*mwit']]_ ("different, other") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Otherness, difference
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#meten|meten]]_
### mekam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [meqɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [meqɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [meqam]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mekam|*mekam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*me-|*me-]]_ ("body") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kam|*kam]]_ ("wash").
> ¹ To bathe
### mekib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mekib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mekɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [mekɪb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mekip|*mekip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*me-|*me-]]_ ("body") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kip|*kip]]_ ("squirt").
> ¹ To urinate
### menaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [menɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [menɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [menaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*menaw|*menaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*me-|*me-]]_ ("body") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naw|*naw]]_ ("clothes").
> ¹ To wear
### menüb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [menyb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [menʏb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [menʏb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*menǖp|*menǖp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*me-|*me-]]_ ("body") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nǖp|*nǖp]]_ ("wrap").
> ¹ Belt
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#minöb|minöb]]_
### metaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [metɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [medɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [medaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*metaw|*metaw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*me-|*me-]]_ ("body") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taw|*taw]]_ ("carry").
> ¹ To carry on the back
### mihwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mixʷɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [miɸɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [miɸa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mihwa|*mihwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mih|*mih]]_ ("live") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Alive, as of a person; ² Free
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#mífa|mífa]]_
### milam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [milɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [milɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [milam]

### miswa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [miswɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [miswɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [miswa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*miswa|*miswa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mis|*mis]]_ ("clear") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wis|*wis]]_ ("transparent").
> ¹ Clear, as of water or an area of land
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#mísva|mísva]]_
### mitös
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mitøs]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [midœs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [midœs]

> ¹ To smoke

### mümüb

### myawa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mjɑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mjɑwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [mjawa]

### myawmö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [mjɑwmø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [mjɑwmœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [mjawmœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmü|*myawmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umü|*umü]]_ ("five"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*maq|*maq]]_ ("repeat").
> ¹ Twenty five (five squared)
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ñomö|ñomö]]_ ("twenty five")

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmmü|*myawmmü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmü|*myawmü]]_ ("twenty five (five squared)") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A calendar year, equal to 250 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ñomö|ñomö]]_
# n
### -na

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-na|*-na]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count longish objects such as fish (dead, for eating), certain fruit, dead bodies, knives and planks of wood
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-na|-na]]_

### nanekwa

### naniw

### naqem

# o
### oban
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [obɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [obɑn]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [oban]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*upwan|*upwan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pwan|*pwan]]_ ("fill").
> ¹ To fill up; ² To pour
### obay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [obɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [obɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [obaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wupay|*wupay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pay|*pay]]_ ("layer").
> ¹ To coat in paint
### okam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oqɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oqɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [oqam]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wukam|*wukam]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kam|*kam]]_ ("wash").
> ¹ To wash, as of clothes
### okit'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [okitʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [okɪtʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [okɪtʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ukit'|*ukit']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kit'|*kit']]_ ("erect, upright").
> ¹ To erect; ² To construct
### okop'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [okopʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [okɔpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [okɔpʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ukup'|*ukup']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kup'|*kup']]_ ("burst, pop").
> ¹ To pop, burst
### ok'ay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oqʼɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oqʼɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [oqʼaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*uq'ay|*uq'ay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'ay|*q'ay]]_ ("fall").
> ¹ To knock down
### ok'i
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [okʼi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [okʼɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [okʼɪ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuk'i|*wuk'i]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'i|*k'i]]_ ("hang, swing").
> ¹ To swing
### olak'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olɑqʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [olɑqʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [olaqʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urlak'|*urlak']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lak'|*lak']]_ ("insert").
> ¹ To insert; ² To drive in, as of a wooden dowel
### olaw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olɑw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [olɑw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [olaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuraw|*wuraw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wu-|*wu-]]_ ("back and forth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*raw|*raw]]_ ("sew, weave").
> ¹ To weave
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#uro|uro]]_
### olay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [olɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [olaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wray|*wray]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*we-|*we-]]_ ("absence of") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ray|*ray]]_ ("be in a place").
> ¹ To be absent

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*uray|*uray]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ray|*ray]]_ ("be in a place").
> ¹ To put in place
### olbal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olbɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫbɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owbaw]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urpal|*urpal]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pal|*pal]]_ ("wax, flow, accumulate").
> ¹ To wax, as of a moon
### olcöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oltʃøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫdʒœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owdʒɔ̃ː]

> ¹ To push
### olhüb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olxʷyb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫɸʏb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owɸʏb]

### olk'öb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olkʼøb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫkʼœb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owkʼœb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urk'üp|*urk'üp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*k'üp|*k'üp]]_ ("spit, vomit").
> ¹ To spit at
### olmay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olmɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫmɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owmaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urmay|*urmay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*may|*may]]_ ("know, remember").
> ¹ To teach; ² To explain
### olmöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olmøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫmœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owmew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urmül|*urmül]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mül|*mül]]_ ("learn, teach").
> ¹ To teach something
### oltil
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oltil]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫdɪɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owdew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urtil|*urtil]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*til|*til]]_ ("approach").

### oltüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [oltym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫdʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owdʊ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*urtǖm|*urtǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ur-|*ur-]]_ ("towards object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖm|*tǖm]]_ ("hand").
> ¹ To give something
### olüt
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [olyt]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [oɫt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [owt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wurǖt|*wurǖt]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wuraw|*wuraw]]_ ("to weave") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Basket
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#út|út]]_
### ombla
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [omblɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ɔ̃mblɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ɔ̃mbla]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umpla|*umpla]]_.
> ¹ [[Ombla]], a small feathered dinosaur
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#onbla|onbla]]_
### omis
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [omis]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [omɪs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [omɪs]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umis|*umis]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mis|*mis]]_ ("clear").
> ¹ To clear out an area
### omö
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [omø]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [omœ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [omœ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umü|*umü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*um|*um]]_ ("five").
> ¹ Five
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#acowmö|acowmö]]_ ("six"), _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#wibowmö|wibowmö]]_ ("seven"), _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#nüɸowmö|nüɸowmö]]_ ("eight"), _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#bixowmö|bixowmö]]_ ("nine")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#umö|umö]]_

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ummü|*ummü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*um|*um]]_ ("five") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle").
> ¹ A major month, equal to 50 days
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-ö|-ö]]_ ("cycle classifier"), [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#umö|umö]]_
### omön
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [omøn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [omœ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [omɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umyün|*umyün]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*u-|*u-]]_ ("causative") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myün|*myün]]_ ("grow, increase").
> ¹ To increase, multiply; ² To build up

### omyawmü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [omjɑwmy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [omjɑwmʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [omjawmʏ]

*num.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ummyawmiü|*ummyawmiü]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*umü|*umü]]_ ("five") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*myawmü|*myawmü]]_ ("twenty five (five squared)") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-i|*-i]]_ ("relational linker").
> ¹ One hundred and twenty five (five cubed)
### onal
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [onɑl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [onɑɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [onaw]

### ot'ag

# ö
### -ö

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*mü|*mü]]_ ("cycle"), from [[Proto-Upic language|Proto-Upic]] _[[Proto-Upic dictionary#\*mu|*mu]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count cyclic objects such as wheels, months and years, as well as generations and things of a reciprocal nature such as transactions
### öb
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [øb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [øb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üp|*üp]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üp|*üp]]_ ("person").
> ¹ Person; ² The [[Öb]] people as a whole
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öb|öb]]_
### öcem
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ødʒɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ødʒɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yücem|*yücem]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yüc|*yüc]]_ ("wish, desire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Wish, desire
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öjen|öjen]]_
### öck'ay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃqʼɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [øtʃqʼɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [øtʃqʼaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücq'ay|*ücq'ay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üc-|*üc-]]_ ("periodically over a long time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*q'ay|*q'ay]]_ ("fall").
> ¹ To set each day, as of the sun or stars
### öcnaen
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃnɑen]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ødʒnɑɛ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ødʒnaj]

*v. imp.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücnaʔen|*ücnaʔen]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-en|*-en]]_ ("impersonal verb") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üc-|*üc-]]_ ("periodically over a long time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*naʔ|*naʔ]]_ ("time").
> ¹ To have time pass
### öcöc'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃøtʃʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ødʒœtʃʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ødʒœtʃʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücyüc'|*ücyüc']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üc-|*üc-]]_ ("periodically over a long time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*kyüc'|*kyüc']]_ ("rise").
> ¹ To rise each day, as of the sun or stars
### öcök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃøk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ødʒœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ødʒœk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücük|*ücük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ü-|*ü-]]_ ("away from object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cük|*cük]]_ ("snap").
> ¹ To snap off
### öcöm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃøm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ødʒœ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ødʒɔ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücüm|*ücüm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ü-|*ü-]]_ ("away from object") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*cüm|*cüm]]_ ("manipulate").
> ¹ To pull
### öcwin
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃwin]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ødʒwɪ̃n]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ødʒwɪ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücwin|*ücwin]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üc-|*üc-]]_ ("periodically over a long time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gwin|*gwin]]_ ("eclipse").
> ¹ The periodic eclipse of Bigmoon by Smallmoon
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öjvin|öjvin]]_

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ücwin|*ücwin]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*üc-|*üc-]]_ ("periodically over a long time") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*win|*win]]_ ("count, hold value").
> ¹ To count days, measure the passing of time
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#öci|öci]]_

ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [øtʃʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [øtʃʼɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [øtʃʼab]

# q
### qanyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑɲɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑɲɑn]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔaɲan]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qanyan|*qanyan]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qyan|*qyan]]_ ("cover").
> ¹ Lid of a container; ² Roof
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qañan|qañan]]_
### qata
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔada]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qata|*qata]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qer|*qer]]_ ("close eyes") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Closed eyes
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qada|qada]]_
### qaüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔaw]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaywǖm|*qaywǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwiw|*qwiw]]_ ("south-easterly monsoon wind") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ The south
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qo|qo]]_
### qawet
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑwt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔawt]

*n.* From _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#hoqaw|hoqaw]]_ ("to mix") + _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#-et|-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Mixture
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qot|qot]]_
### qaylos
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjlos]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjlɔs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajlɔs]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qayrus|*qayrus]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qrus|*qrus]]_ ("day").
> ¹ Daytime
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qelos|qelos]]_
### qaylök
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjløk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjlœk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajlœk]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaylük|*qaylük]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qay-|*qay-]]_ ("downwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*lük|*lük]]_ ("poke").
> ¹ To plant
### qayox
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjoʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajʃ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qayux|*qayux]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qux|*qux]]_ ("sunny").
> ¹ Clear weather
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qex|qex]]_
### qaysol
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjsol]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjsɔɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajsow]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaysur|*qaysur]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qay-|*qay-]]_ ("downwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*sur|*sur]]_ ("submerge").
> ¹ To submerge, bury
### qaytob
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjtob]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjdɔb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajdɔb]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaytup|*qaytup]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qay-|*qay-]]_ ("downwards") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tup|*tup]]_ ("press").
> ¹ To press down on
### qayuma
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjumɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjmɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajma]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaywǖma|*qaywǖma]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaywǖm|*qaywǖm]]_ ("the south").
> ¹ Southwards
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qema|qema]]_
### qaywiw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjwiw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjwɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajwew]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qaywiw|*qaywiw]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qwiw|*qwiw]]_ ("south-easterly monsoon wind").
> ¹ Monsoon season
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qevö|qevö]]_
### qayxil
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔɑjʃil]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔɑjʃɪɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔajʃew]

### qelqel
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔelʔel]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔeɫʔɛɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔewʔew]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qerqer|*qerqer]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qer|*qer]]_ ("close eyes") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("directionless intransitive").
> ¹ To close the eyes
### quta
ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔudɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔuda]

*stat.* From [[Xiri]] _[[Xiri dictionary#a’uda|a’uda]]_ ("power"), from [[Proto-Xiric language|Proto-Xiric]] _[[Proto-Xiric dictionary#\*a’uta|*a’uta]]_.
> ¹ Strong; ² Powerful
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qúda|qúda]]_
### qütwa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ʔytwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʔydwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʔydwa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qǖtwa|*qǖtwa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*qǖt|*qǖt]]_ ("empty, hollow") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-u|*-u]]_ ("stativiser").
> ¹ Empty, hollow
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#qídva|qídva]]_

### sotcaic
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [sottʃɑitʃ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [sottʃɑjtʃ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [sottʃajtʃ]

> ¹ A green comet which appears in Winter's sky every few centuries

### tanyag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑɲɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑɲɑɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [taɲaɴ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tanyag|*tanyag]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<an>|*<an>]]_ ("instrument") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyag|*tyag]]_ ("bone").
> ¹ Bone
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dañan|dañan]]_
### taset
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑset]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑsɛt]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tasɛt]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taset|*taset]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tas|*tas]]_ ("dry") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Dried meat
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#daset|daset]]_
### tasta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑstɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑstɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tasta]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tasta|*tasta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tas|*tas]]_ ("dry") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Dried out
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dasta|dasta]]_
### tata
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑdɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tada]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taʔtaʔ|*taʔtaʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taʔ|*taʔ]]_ ("tooth") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Tooth (of a person)
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dada|dada]]_
### tawa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑwɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑwɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tawa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tawa|*tawa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taw|*taw]]_ ("carry").
> ¹ Heavy
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dova|dova]]_
### taya
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑjɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑjɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [taja]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tayaʔ|*tayaʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taʔ|*taʔ]]_ ("tooth").
> ¹ Gum (of teeth)
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#deya|deya]]_
### tayag
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑjɑɴ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑjɑɴ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tajaɴ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tayyag|*tayyag]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*<ay>|*<ay>]]_ ("circumstance") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tyag|*tyag]]_ ("bone").
> ¹ Ribcage, chest

### tayay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tɑjɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɑjɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tajaj]

*procl.*
> ¹ First person possessive
### teqta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [teʔtɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [teʔtɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [teʔta]

### ticok'

### tikis

### tiköm

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-tik'|*-tik']]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count small round clustering things such as seeds, grains, pebbles, berries, small eggs and stars
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-dik|-dik]]_
### tilös
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tiløs]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tiɫs]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tews]

### tiüm

### tiyu

### -to

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-tu|*-tu]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count large land animals such as [[Ugo]], [[Mlomlo]], [[Yunam]] and [[K'ak'oh]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-do|-do]]_
### togtog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [toŋtoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tɔ̃ndɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tɔ̃ndɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tugtug|*tugtug]]_.
> ¹ [[Togtog]], a tall [[Wug]], similar to the springbok or gerenuk
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dondon|dondon]]_
### tosi
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tosi]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tosɪ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tosɪ]

### töliw
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøliw]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tølɪw]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tølew]

> ¹ To tie together
### tölüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tølym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tølʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tølʊ̃ː]

### tömab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tømɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tømɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tømab]

### töminet

### tömön

### tönal

### tötob
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøtob]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tødɔb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tødɔb]

### tötyom

### töwik'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tøwikʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tøwkʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tewkʼ]

### töwin

### tük
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tyk]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tyk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tyk]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖk|*tǖk]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*taw|*taw]]_ ("carry") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ek|*-ek]]_ ("animate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Female animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dík|dík]]_
### tüka
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tyqɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tyqɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tyqa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖka|*tǖka]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖk|*tǖk]]_ ("female animal").
> ¹ Female, of animals
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#díka|díka]]_
### tümib
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tymib]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tymɪb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tymɪb]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖmip|*tǖmip]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖm|*tǖm]]_ ("hand") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ip|*ip]]_ ("thin, narrow").
> ¹ Wrist
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dímib|dímib]]_
### tümnim
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tymnim]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tynɪ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tynɪ̃ː]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖmnim|*tǖmnim]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖm|*tǖm]]_ ("hand") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*nim|*nim]]_ ("build").
> ¹ To create, build (by hand)
### tümog
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tymoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tymɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tymɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖmug|*tǖmug]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖm|*tǖm]]_ ("hand") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ug|*-ug]]_ ("augmentative").
> ¹ A rake used to harvest [[cimcim]]
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dímon|dímon]]_
### tümtüm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tymtym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʏ̃ndʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʊ̃ndʊ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖmtǖm|*tǖmtǖm]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tǖm|*tǖm]]_ ("hand") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Hand
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#dundun|dundun]]_
### tüp'
[typʼ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tüyip'|*tüyip']]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*tü-|*tü-]]_ ("together") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yip'|*yip']]_ ("pinch, squeeze").
> ¹ To pinch
### twimab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [twimɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [twimɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [twimab]

### twökem

### twökim

### twökya

> ¹ Hook shaped; ² Bent

### tyomek
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [comek]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [comɛk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [comɛk]

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#jömek|jömek]]_
### tyomta

### tyomtyag

# t'
### t'aba
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼɑbɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼɑbɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼaba]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'apa|*t'apa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ap|*t'ap]]_ ("smooth").
> ¹ Smooth, slippery
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#taba|taba]]_
### t'ak'og
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼɑkʼoŋ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼɑkʼɔ̃ŋ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼakʼɔ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'aq'ug|*t'aq'ug]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'aq'|*t'aq']]_ ("shell") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ug|*-ug]]_ ("augmentative").
> ¹ [[K'ak'oh]], a giant snail endemic to [[T'ugü]]
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#k'ak'ohümi|k'ak'ohümi]]_ ("wagon house")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#takon|takon]]_
### t'anik
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼɑnik]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼɑnɪk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼanɪk]

> ¹ Knife
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#tanik|tanik]]_
### t'anök'

> ¹ To cut up into pieces, as of fabric or leafy vegetables
### t'ökt'ök'

### t'uc'ah

> ¹ To destroy
### t'ugü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [tʼuŋy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [tʼuŋʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [tʼuŋʏ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ūgǖʔ|*t'ūgǖʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*t'ū-|*t'ū-]]_ ("whole, entire") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*gǖʔ|*gǖʔ]]_ ("land").
> ¹ The [[T'ugü]] river basin, the entire world known to the [[Öb]] before contact with other cultures
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#túgö|túgö]]_

### t'uxiw

# u
### -u

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ū|*-ū]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count structureless or abstract objects such as thoughts, colours and sounds
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-u|-u]]_
### ua
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [uɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ua]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wūʔa|*wūʔa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wūʔ|*wūʔ]]_ ("good").
> ¹ Good, right; ² Fortunate
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úva|úva]]_
### ubak
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubɑq]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubɑq]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubaq]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpak|*ūpak]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pak|*pak]]_ ("animal").
> ¹ Any wild land animal
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úbak|úbak]]_
### ubay
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubɑj]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubɑj]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubaj]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūppay|*ūppay]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*pay|*pay]]_ ("layer").
> ¹ To layer on, as of paint

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūpway|*ūpway]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūp-|*ūp-]]_ ("surface") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*way|*way]]_ ("apply").
> ¹ To apply dye or varnish; ² To treat a wound
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úbe|úbe]]_ ("to lacquer, apply")
### ubgü
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubŋy]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubŋʏ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubŋʏ]

### ubliw

### ublüm

### uböt

### ubt'ab
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubtʼɑb]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubtʼɑb]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubtʼab]

### ubt'ik

> ¹ To pound flat
### ubyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ubjɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ubjɑn]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ubjan]

### ugo
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [uŋo]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [uŋɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [uŋɔ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ūgu|*ūgu]]_.
> ¹ [[Ugo]], a large domesticated ungulate used as a draft animal, similar to cattle
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#úgo|úgo]]_
### -uk

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-ūk|*-ūk]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count objects with a branching structure such as trees, pieces of [[Cimcim#Ökya cimcim|ökya cimcim]] and lightning bolts
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-uk|-uk]]_

> ¹ To roll out

### ükis

### ülan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ylɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylɑn]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ylan]

Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖtyan|*ǖtyan]]_ ("near"), [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*ǖyan|*ǖyan]]_ ("inside").
> ¹ To be on the surface of
### ülap'
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ylɑpʼ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ylɑpʼ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ylapʼ]

### üm
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ym]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ʏ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ʊ̃ː]

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#un|un]]_

### üta
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yda]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖta|*yǖta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("enclose") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Enclosed
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ída|ída]]_

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yǖta|*yǖta]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yaw|*yaw]]_ ("bend") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-et|*-et]]_ ("resultative, perfective").
> ¹ Bent, curved
> **Derivatives:** _[[Low Alöbi dictionary#üt|üt]]_ ("bow")
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#ída|ída]]_
### ütöl
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ytøl]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [ydœɫ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [ydew]

> ¹ To be in front of
### ütyan
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [ycɑn]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [yɟɑn]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [yɟan]

> ¹ To be within reach; ² To be directly next to

### wit'em
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [witʼem]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [witʼɛ̃m]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [witʼɛ̃ː]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wit'em|*wit'em]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wit'|*wit']]_ ("different, other") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-em|*-em]]_ ("inanimate object nominaliser").
> ¹ Other thing
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#víten|víten]]_
### wixa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wiʃɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wiʃɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wiʃa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wīxa|*wīxa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wīx|*wīx]]_ ("sacred, shining"). Perhaps related to [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*plīxma|*plīxma]]_ ("shining").
> ¹ Sacred; ² Relating to light in spiritual or theological contexts
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#víxa|víxa]]_
### -wo

*suff.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*-wu|*-wu]]_.
> ¹ Numeral classifier used to count hollow objects such as baskets, barrels, bags, houses, caves, and some shells
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#-vo|-vo]]_
### wöa
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wøɑ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wøɑ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wøa]

*stat.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wüʔa|*wüʔa]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*wüʔ|*wüʔ]]_ ("omen, luck").
> ¹ Lucky, as of a person
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#vöya|vöya]]_
### wöxik
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [wøʃik]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [wøʃɪk]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [wøʃɪk]

> ¹ Bird of prey
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#vöxik|vöxik]]_

> ¹ To bend, curve

### yabek

> ¹ Insect larva

> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúvek|yúvek]]_
### yunam
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [junɑm]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [junɑm]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [junam]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūnam|*yūnam]]_.
> ¹ [[Yunam]], a large ungulate, similar to antelopes
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúnan|yúnan]]_
### yup'üh
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [jupʼyxʷ]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jupʼʏɸ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jupʼʏɸ]

*v.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūp'ǖh|*yūp'ǖh]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*p'ǖh|*p'ǖh]]_ ("swarm").
> ¹ To swarm; ² To envelope
### yuso
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juso]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jusɔ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jusɔ]

*pron.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūsu|*yūsu]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*i-|*i-]]_ ("singular") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*usu|*usu]]_ ("second person").
> ¹ Second person singular
### yuyu
ᴇᴀʀʟʏ [juju]; ᴍᴀᴛᴜʀᴇ [jujʊ]; ᴛʀᴀɴꜱɪᴛɪᴏɴᴀʟ [jujʊ]

*n.* From [[Proto-Öbic language|Proto-Öbic]] _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔyūʔ|*yūʔyūʔ]]_, from _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*yūʔ|*yūʔ]]_ ("scale") + _[[Proto-Öbic dictionary#\*~|*~]]_ ("specifier").
> ¹ Scales, as of fish or a lizard
> **Descendants:** [[Möxali]] _[[Möxali dictionary#yúyu|yúyu]]_
